# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
find all natural number factors of the given number
63 ^Uth8v2wz

Divisibility tests, also known as divisibility rules, are shortcut methods used to quickly determine whether one number can be divided evenly by another without actually performing the division. These rules rely on examining the digits or certain properties of the number, rather than doing full calculations. ^7UhbxBkO

For example: ^bsUeZxrG

A number is divisible by 2 if its last digit is even (0, 2, 4, 6, or 8). ^eBAHJuKN

A number is divisible by 3 if the sum of its digits is divisible by 3. ^9o9KKFKg

A number is divisible by 5 if its last digit is 0 or 5. ^liRz0hC3

priime factorization of ^chN6h18e

prime factorization of
 ^ERACd7ux

Deffie-Hellman-Merkle key exchange ^r2TtKoHO

Try values or use the Extended Euclidean Algorithm ^0iWCJJYY
